[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-m[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/CellFormatter.jav[0m[1;92ma:64[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m75[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:        double minVal = [0m[1;36m1.0[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:        double currDenom = [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - 1d;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:        double currNum = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - 1d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; i > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:            for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i2 = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - 1d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; i2 >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i2--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mminVal >= [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi2 [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi - decPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:                    currDenom = i;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:                    currNum = i2;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:                    minVal = [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m i2 [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m i - decPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify root cause:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The nested loops in CellFormatter.format [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m iterate over all [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpossible numerator/denominator pairs up to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength, where denomLength is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtaken directly from the pattern group [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This can lead to trillions of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterations and effectively hang the process on certain crafted inputs.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve desired functionality:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still want to support fraction formatting for reasonable denominator [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlengths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. up to [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but reject or short-circuit extreme cases to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoid DoS.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implement Denominator‐Length Cap:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Introduce a private static constant in CellFormatter:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final int MAX_DENOM_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after computing denomLength [0m[1;39m([0m[39moriginal line [0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add a guard:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenomLength > MAX_DENOM_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m too expensive to compute; skip fraction formatting[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return cell;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures inputs requesting huge denominators simply bypass the expensive [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfraction algorithm.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implement Early Exit on Exact Match:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Wrap the nested loops in a labeled outer loop and break both loops when an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexact match [0m[1;39m([0m[39mminVal == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is found. This accelerates the common case when the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfractional part can be represented exactly.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Example:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       outer:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = max; i > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i2 = max; i2 >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i2--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               double diff = [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi2 [0m[35m/[0m[39m i - decPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdiff <= minVal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   currDenom = i;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   currNum = i2;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   minVal = diff;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mminVal == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       break outer;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. No other code changes:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not touch TextAndCSVParser or any fuzz harness or tests.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other logic and formatting behavior remains intact for typical use cases.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Capping denomLength at [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m limits the worst-case loops to [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m×[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmillion iterations, which completes quickly even under fuzzing timeouts. [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Early-exit on exact matches further reduces average work.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Skipping formatting on extreme denom lengths still returns the original cell [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent, avoiding silent data loss. This strategy trades off fraction formatting [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor DoS protection only on pathological inputs, preserving correct behavior for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpractical patterns.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Side-effects and mitigation:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Cases where users explicitly request denominator patterns longer than [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m digits[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill fall back to returning the raw cell. If stricter fraction formatting is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired in such scenarios, the MAX_DENOM_LENGTH constant can be tuned upward [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m after verifying performance limits.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on CSV parsing state machine or other parser modules.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Code references:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m/parser/csv/CellFormatter.java around lines [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[39m.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis patch addresses the hang without altering the external API, fuzz harness, or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests, and restores normal fuzzer progress under all inputs. [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
